## AllNodesDistanceKinBinaryTree

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/AllNodesDistanceKinBinaryTree.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nclass AllNodesDistanceKinBinaryTree {\n    val parentMap = mutableMapOf<TreeNode, TreeNode?>()  // To store parent references\n\n    fun distanceK(root: TreeNode?, target: TreeNode?, k: Int): List<Int> {\n        val result = mutableListOf<Int>()\n\n        // Helper function to perform DFS and populate parent map, then find target\n        fun dfs(node: TreeNode?, parent: TreeNode?) {\n            if (node == null) return\n            parentMap[node] = parent\n            if (node == target) collectNodesAtDistanceK(node, k, mutableSetOf(), result)\n            dfs(node.left, node)\n            dfs(node.right, node)\n        }\n\n        // Start DFS from the root to populate parentMap and find the target\n        dfs(root, null)\n        return result\n    }\n\n    // Function to collect nodes at distance K from the target node\n    private fun collectNodesAtDistanceK(node: TreeNode?, k: Int, visited: MutableSet<TreeNode>, result: MutableList<Int>) {\n        if (node == null || visited.contains(node)) return\n        visited.add(node)\n\n        when (k) {\n            0 -> result.add(node.`val`)  // If distance is 0, add node's value to result\n            else -> {\n                collectNodesAtDistanceK(node.left, k - 1, visited, result)\n                collectNodesAtDistanceK(node.right, k - 1, visited, result)\n                collectNodesAtDistanceK(parentMap[node], k - 1, visited, result)  // Explore parent node\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}"  java="class AllNodesDistanceKinBinaryTree {\n    val parentMap = mutableMapOf<TreeNode, TreeNode?>()  // To store parent references\n\n    public static void $1(root: TreeNode?, target: TreeNode?, k): List<Int> {\n        val result = mutableListOf<Int>()\n\n        // Helper function to perform DFS and populate parent map, then find target\n        public static void $1(node: TreeNode?, parent: TreeNode?) {\n            if (node == null) return\n            parentMap[node] = parent\n            if (node == target) collectNodesAtDistanceK(node, k, mutableSetOf(), result)\n            dfs(node.left, node)\n            dfs(node.right, node)\n        }\n\n        // Start DFS from the root to populate parentMap and find the target\n        dfs(root, null)\n        return result\n    }\n\n    // Function to collect nodes at distance K from the target node\n    private public static void $1(node: TreeNode?, k, visited: MutableSet<TreeNode>, result: MutableList<Int>) {\n        if (node == null || visited.contains(node)) return\n        visited.add(node)\n\n        when (k) {\n            0 -> result.add(node.`val`)  // If distance is 0, add node's value to result\n            else -> {\n                collectNodesAtDistanceK(node.left, k - 1, visited, result)\n                collectNodesAtDistanceK(node.right, k - 1, visited, result)\n                collectNodesAtDistanceK(parentMap[node], k - 1, visited, result)  // Explore parent node\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}"  python="class AllNodesDistanceKinBinaryTree {\n    $1 = mutableMapOf<TreeNode, TreeNode?>()  // To store parent references\n\n    def $1(root: TreeNode?, target: TreeNode?, k: int): List<Int> {\n        $1 = mutableListOf<Int>()\n\n        // Helper function to perform DFS and populate parent map, then find target\n        def $1(node: TreeNode?, parent: TreeNode?) {\n            if (node == None) return\n            parentMap[node] = parent\n            if (node == target) collectNodesAtDistanceK(node, k, mutableSetOf(), result)\n            dfs(node.left, node)\n            dfs(node.right, node)\n        }\n\n        // Start DFS from the root to populate parentMap and find the target\n        dfs(root, None)\n        return result\n    }\n\n    // Function to collect nodes at distance K from the target node\n    private def $1(node: TreeNode?, k: int, visited: MutableSet<TreeNode>, result: MutableList<Int>) {\n        if (node == None || visited.contains(node)) return\n        visited.add(node)\n\n        when (k) {\n            0 -> result.add(node.`val`)  // If distance is 0, add node's value to result\n            else -> {\n                collectNodesAtDistanceK(node.left, k - 1, visited, result)\n                collectNodesAtDistanceK(node.right, k - 1, visited, result)\n                collectNodesAtDistanceK(parentMap[node], k - 1, visited, result)  // Explore parent node\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}"  rust="class AllNodesDistanceKinBinaryTree {\n    val parentMap = mutableMapOf<TreeNode, TreeNode?>()  // To store parent references\n\n    fn $1(root: TreeNode?, target: TreeNode?, k -> i32): List<Int> {\n        val result = mutableListOf<Int>()\n\n        // Helper function to perform DFS and populate parent map, then find target\n        fn $1(node: TreeNode?, parent: TreeNode?) {\n            if (node == None) return\n            parentMap[node] = parent\n            if (node == target) collectNodesAtDistanceK(node, k, mutableSetOf(), result)\n            dfs(node.left, node)\n            dfs(node.right, node)\n        }\n\n        // Start DFS from the root to populate parentMap and find the target\n        dfs(root, None)\n        return result\n    }\n\n    // Function to collect nodes at distance K from the target node\n    private fn $1(node: TreeNode?, k -> i32, visited: MutableSet<TreeNode>, result: MutableList<Int>) {\n        if (node == None || visited.contains(node)) return\n        visited.add(node)\n\n        when (k) {\n            0 -> result.add(node.`val`)  // If distance is 0, add node's value to result\n            else -> {\n                collectNodesAtDistanceK(node.left, k - 1, visited, result)\n                collectNodesAtDistanceK(node.right, k - 1, visited, result)\n                collectNodesAtDistanceK(parentMap[node], k - 1, visited, result)  // Explore parent node\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}"  cpp="class AllNodesDistanceKinBinaryTree {\n    auto $1 = mutableMapOf<TreeNode, TreeNode?>()  // To store parent references\n\n    $1(root: TreeNode?, target: TreeNode?, k): List<Int> {\n        auto $1 = mutableListOf<Int>()\n\n        // Helper function to perform DFS and populate parent map, then find target\n        $1(node: TreeNode?, parent: TreeNode?) {\n            if (node == nullptr) return\n            parentMap[node] = parent\n            if (node == target) collectNodesAtDistanceK(node, k, mutableSetOf(), result)\n            dfs(node.left, node)\n            dfs(node.right, node)\n        }\n\n        // Start DFS from the root to populate parentMap and find the target\n        dfs(root, nullptr)\n        return result\n    }\n\n    // Function to collect nodes at distance K from the target node\n    private $1(node: TreeNode?, k, visited: MutableSet<TreeNode>, result: MutableList<Int>) {\n        if (node == nullptr || visited.contains(node)) return\n        visited.add(node)\n\n        when (k) {\n            0 -> result.add(node.`val`)  // If distance is 0, add node's value to result\n            else -> {\n                collectNodesAtDistanceK(node.left, k - ## BInaryTreeInOrderTraversalIterative

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nclass BInaryTreeInOrderTraversalIterative {\n    fun inorderTraversal(root: TreeNode?): List<Int> {\n        val stack = ArrayDeque<TreeNode>()\n        val result = mutableListOf<Int>()\n        var current = root\n\n        while (current != null || stack.isNotEmpty()) {\n            // Traverse to the leftmost node\n            while (current != ## BalancedBinaryTree

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/BalancedBinaryTree.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nimport kotlin.math.abs\n\nclass BalancedBinaryTree {\n    fun isBalanced(root: TreeNode?): Boolean {\n        fun checkHeight(node: TreeNode?): Int {\n            if (node == null) return 0\n\n            val leftHeight = checkHeight(node.left)\n            val rightHeight = checkHeight(node.right)\n\n            // If subtree is unbalanced, return -1 to signal it\n            if (leftHeight == -1 || rightHeight == -1 || abs(leftHeight - rightHeight) > 1) {\n                return -1\n            }\n\n            // Return the height of the tree rooted at this node\n            return 1 + maxOf(leftHeight, rightHeight)\n        }\n\n        return checkHeight(root) != -1\n    }\n}"  java="class BalancedBinaryTree {\n    public static void $1(root: TreeNode?) {\n        public static void $1(node: TreeNode?) {\n            if (node == null) return 0\n\n            val leftHeight = checkHeight(node.left)\n            val rightHeight = checkHeight(node.right)\n\n            // If subtree is unbalanced, return -1 to signal it\n            if (leftHeight == -1 || rightHeight == -1 || abs(leftHeight - rightHeight) > 1) {\n                return -1\n            }\n\n            // Return the height of the tree rooted at this node\n            return 1 + maxOf(leftHeight, rightHeight)\n        }\n\n        return checkHeight(root) != -1\n    }\n}"  python="class BalancedBinaryTree {\n    def $1(root: TreeNode?): bool {\n        def $1(node: TreeNode?): int {\n            if (node == None) return 0\n\n            $1 = checkHeight(node.left)\n            $1 = checkHeight(node.right)\n\n            // If subtree is unbalanced, return -1 to signal it\n            if (leftHeight == -1 || rightHeight == -1 || abs(leftHeight - rightHeight) > 1) {\n                return -1\n            }\n\n            // Return the height of the tree rooted at this node\n            return 1 + max(leftHeight, rightHeight)\n        }\n\n        return checkHeight(root) != -1\n    }\n}"  rust="class BalancedBinaryTree {\n    fn $1(root: TreeNode?) -> bool {\n        fn $1(node: TreeNode?) -> i32 {\n            if (node == None) return 0\n\n            val leftHeight = checkHeight(node.left)\n            val rightHeight = checkHeight(node.right)\n\n            // If subtree is unbalanced, return -1 to signal it\n            if (leftHeight == -1 || rightHeight == -1 || abs(leftHeight - rightHeight) > 1) {\n                return -1\n            }\n\n            // Return the height of the tree rooted at this node\n            return 1 + max(leftHeight, rightHeight)\n        }\n\n        return checkHeight(root) != -1\n    }\n}"  cpp="class BalancedBinaryTree {\n    $1(root: TreeNode?) {\n        $1(node: TreeNode?) {\n            if (node == nullptr) return 0\n\n            auto $1 = checkHeight(node.left)\n            auto $1 = checkHeight(node.right)\n\n            // If subtree is unbalanced, return -1 to signal it\n            if (leftHeight == -1 || rightHeight == -1 || abs(leftHeight - ## BinaryTreeLevelOrderTraversal

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nimport java.util.*\nimport kotlin.collections.ArrayList\n\n\nclass BinaryTreeLevelOrderTraversal {\n    fun levelOrder(root: TreeNode?):            }\n\n            result.add(lst)\n        }\n        return result\n    }\n}"  java="class BinaryTreeLevelOrderTraversal {\n    public static void $1(root: TreeNode?): List<List<Int>> {\n ## BinaryTreeMaximumPathSum

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/BinaryTreeMaximumPathSum.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nclass BinaryTreeMaximumPathSum {\n    fun maxPathSum(root: TreeNode?): Int {\n        var ans = Int.MIN_VALUE\n        fun getMaxPathSum(node: ## BinaryTreeVerticalOrderTraversal_WithoutSorting

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/BinaryTreeVerticalOrderTraversal_WithoutSorting.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nimport java.util.*\n\nclass BinaryTreeVerticalOrderTraversal_WithoutSorting {\n    data class VerticalIndex(val node: TreeNode, val verticalIndex: Int)\n\n    fun verticalOrder(root: TreeNode?): List<List<Int>> {\n        if (root == null) return emptyList()\n\n        val columnTable = mutableMapOf<Int, MutableList<Int>>()\n        var minColumn = 0\n        var maxColumn = 0\n\n        val queue: Queue<VerticalIndex> = LinkedList()\n        queue.offer(VerticalIndex(root, 0))\n\n        while (queue.isNotEmpty()) {\n            val (node, column) = queue.poll()\n\n            columnTable.computeIfAbsent(column) { mutableListOf() }.add(node.`val`)\n\n            // Update min and max column indices\n            minColumn = minOf(minColumn, column)\n            maxColumn = maxOf(maxColumn, column)\n\n            node.left?.let { queue.offer(VerticalIndex(it, column - ## BinaryTreeZigZagLevelOrderTraversal

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nimport java.util.*\n\nclass BinaryTreeZigZagLevelOrderTraversal {\n    data class IndexedNode(var node: TreeNode?, var index: Int)\n\n    fun ## BoundaryOfBinaryTree

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/BoundaryOfBinaryTree.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nclass BoundaryOfBinaryTree {\n    fun boundaryOfBinaryTree(root: TreeNode?): List<Int> {\n        val result = mutableListOf<Int>()\n        if (root == null) return result\n\n        // Step 1: Add the root node\n        result.add(root.`val`)\n\n        // Step 2: Add the left boundary (excluding leaves)\n        addLeftBoundary(root.left, result)\n\n        // Step 3: Add all leaf nodes (excluding root if it is a leaf)\n        addLeaves(root, result, isRoot = true)\n\n        // Step 4: Add the right boundary (excluding leaves, in reverse order)\n        val rightBoundary = mutableListOf<Int>()\n        addRightBoundary(root.right, rightBoundary)\n        result.addAll(rightBoundary.reversed())\n\n        return result\n    }\n\n    private fun addLeftBoundary(node: TreeNode?, result: MutableList<Int>) {\n        var current = node\n        while (current != null) {\n            // Don't add leaf nodes to the left boundary\n            if (current.left != null || current.right != null) {\n                result.add(current.`val`)\n            }\n            // Move down the left child, or the right if left is null\n            current = current.left ?: current.right\n        }\n    }\n\n    private fun addLeaves(node: TreeNode?, result: MutableList<Int>, isRoot: Boolean) {\n        if (node == null) return\n        // If it's a leaf node and it's not the root, add it to the result\n        if (node.left == null && node.right == null && !isRoot) {\n            result.add(node.`val`)\n            return\n        }\n        // Otherwise, continue the traversal for both subtrees\n        addLeaves(node.left, result, isRoot = false)\n        addLeaves(node.right, result, isRoot = false)\n    }\n\n    private fun addRightBoundary(node: TreeNode?, result: MutableList<Int>) {\n        var current = node\n        while (current != null) {\n            // Don't add leaf nodes to the right boundary\n            if (current.left != null || current.right != null) {\n                result.add(current.`val`)\n            }\n            // Move down the right child, or the left if right is null\n            current = current.right ?: current.left\n        }\n    }\n}\n"  java="class BoundaryOfBinaryTree {\n    public static void $1(root: TreeNode?): List<Int> {\n        val result = mutableListOf<Int>()\n        if (root == null) return result\n\n        // Step 1: Add the root node\n        result.add(root.`val`)\n\n        // Step 2: Add the left boundary (excluding leaves)\n        addLeftBoundary(root.left, result)\n\n        // Step 3: Add all leaf nodes (excluding root if it is a leaf)\n        addLeaves(root, result, isRoot = true)\n\n        // Step 4: Add the right boundary (excluding leaves, in reverse order)\n        val rightBoundary = mutableListOf<Int>()\n        addRightBoundary(root.right, rightBoundary)\n        result.addAll(rightBoundary.reversed())\n\n        return result\n    }\n\n    private public static void $1(node: TreeNode?, result: MutableList<Int>) {\n        var current = node\n        while ## ConstructBinaryTreeFromInorderAndPostOrderTraversal

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/ConstructBinaryTreeFromInorderAndPostOrderTraversal.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nclass ConstructBinaryTreeFromInorderAndPostOrderTraversal {\n    fun buildTree(inorder: IntArray, postorder: IntArray): TreeNode? {\n        // Build Inverted InOrder Index Map\n        val rootIndices = mutableMapOf<Int, Int>()\n        inorder.forEachIndexed { index, value -> rootIndices[value] = index }\n\n        var postIndex = postorder.size - 1\n\n        fun buildTree(left: Int, right: Int): TreeNode? {\n            return when {\n                left > right -> null\n                else -> {\n                    val rootVal = postorder[postIndex--]\n                    TreeNode(rootVal).apply {\n                        this.right = buildTree(rootIndices[rootVal]!! + 1, right)  // Build right subtree first\n                        this.left = buildTree(left, rootIndices[rootVal]!! - 1)    // Build left subtree\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        return buildTree(0, inorder.size - 1)\n    }\n}\n"  java="class ConstructBinaryTreeFromInorderAndPostOrderTraversal {\n    public static void $1(inorder: IntArray, postorder: IntArray): TreeNode? {% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nclass ConstructBinaryTreeFromString {\n    fun str2tree(s: String): TreeNode? {\n        if (s.isEmpty()) return null\n\n        return buildTree(s, 0).first // We are only interested in the tree root, not the index\n    }\n\n    private fun buildTree(s: String, i: Int): Pair<TreeNode?, Int> {\n        if (i >= s.length) return Pair(null, i)\n\n        var currentIndex = i\n        val start = currentIndex\n        if (s[currentIndex] == '-') currentIndex++  // Handle negative numbers\n        while (currentIndex < s.length && s[currentIndex].isDigit()) currentIndex++  // Skip over digits\n        val valStr = s.substring(start, currentIndex)\n        val root = TreeNode(valStr.toInt())\n\n        // Check for left child (subtree)\n        if (currentIndex < s.length && s[currentIndex] == '(') {\n            currentIndex++  // Skip '('\n            val leftResult = buildTree(s, currentIndex)\n            root.left = leftResult.first\n            currentIndex = leftResult.second  // Update index after processing left subtree\n            if (currentIndex < s.length && s[currentIndex] == ')') currentIndex++  // Skip ')'\n        }\n\n        // Check for right child (subtree)\n        if (currentIndex < s.length && s[currentIndex] == '(') {\n            currentIndex++  // Skip '('\n            val rightResult = buildTree(s, currentIndex)\n            root.right = rightResult.first\n            currentIndex = rightResult.second  // Update index after processing right subtree\n            if (currentIndex < s.length && s[currentIndex] == ')') currentIndex++  // Skip ')'\n        }\n\n        return root to currentIndex  // Return the node and the updated index\n    }\n}\n"  java="class ConstructBinaryTreeFromString {\n    public static void $1(s): TreeNode? ## CountNodeEqualsAverage

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/CountNodeEqualsAverage.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nclass TreeNode(var `val`: Int) {\n    var left: TreeNode? = null\n    var right: TreeNode? = null\n}\n\ndata class Result (val sum: Int, val count: Int)\n\nclass CountNodeEqualsAverage {\n    var count = 0\n\n    fun averageOfSubtree(root: TreeNode?): Int {\n        postOrder(root)\n        return count;\n    }\n\n    private fun postOrder(root: TreeNode?): Result {\n        if (root == null)\n            return Result(sum = 0, count = 0)\n\n        val left = postOrder(root.left)\n        val right = postOrder(root.right)\n\n        val nodeSum = root.`val` + left.sum + right.sum\n        val nodeCount = 1 + left.count + right.count\n        if ( root.`val` == nodeSum/nodeCount)\n            count++\n\n        return Result(sum = nodeSum, count = nodeCount)\n    }\n}"  java="class TreeNode(var `val`) {\n    var left: TreeNode? ## DiameterOfNArrayTree

## LongestPathWithDifferentAdjacentCharacters

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nclass LongestPathWithDifferentAdjacentCharacters {\n    fun longestPath(parent: IntArray, s: String): Int {\n        val children = ## LongestUnivaluePath

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/LongestUnivaluePath.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nclass LongestUnivaluePath {\n\n    fun longestUnivaluePath(root: TreeNode?): Int {\n        var maxLength = 0\n        fun dfs(node: TreeNode?): Int {\n            if (node == null) return 0\n\n            // Get the maximum univalue chain from both left and right\n            val left = dfs(node.left)\n            val right = dfs(node.right)\n\n            // Compute the branch lengthes if\n            val currentLeft = if (node.left?.`val` == node.`val`) left + 1 else 0\n            val currentRight = if (node.right?.`val` == node.`val`) right + 1 else 0\n\n            // Take maximum of max found so far , OD\n            maxLength = maxOf(maxLength, currentLeft + currentRight)\n\n            // We can only propagate the maximum branch chain b/w left and right\n            return maxOf(currentLeft, currentRight)\n        }\n\n        dfs(root)\n        return maxLength\n    }\n}"  java="class LongestUnivaluePath {\n\n    public static void $1(root: TreeNode?) {\n        var maxLength = 0\n        public static void $1(node: TreeNode?) {\n            if (node == null) return 0\n\n            // Get the maximum univalue return max(currentLeft, currentRight)\n        }\n\n        dfs(root)\n        return maxLength\n    }\n}"  rust="class LongestUnivaluePath {\n\n    fn $1(root: TreeNode?) -> i32 {\n        var maxLength = 0\n        fn $1(node: TreeNode?) -> i32 {\n            if (node == None) return 0\n\n            // Get the maximum univalue chain from both left and right\n            val left = chain from both left and right\n            auto $1 = dfs(node.left)\n            auto $1 = dfs(node.right)\n\n            // Compute the branch lengthes if\n            auto $1 = if (node.left?.`val` ## LowestCommonAncestor

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/LowestCommonAncestor.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nclass LowestCommonAncestor {\n    fun lowestCommonAncestor(root: TreeNode?, p: TreeNode?, q: TreeNode?): TreeNode? {\n        if (root == null || root === p || root === q) return root\n\n        val left = lowestCommonAncestor(root.left, p, q)\n        val right = lowestCommonAncestor(root.right, p, q)\n\n        return if (left != null && right != null) root else left ?: right\n\n    }\n}"  java="class LowestCommonAncestor {\n    public static void $1(root: TreeNode?, p: TreeNode?, q: TreeNode?): TreeNode? {\n        if (root == null || root === p || root === q) return root\n\n        val left = lowestCommonAncestor(root.left, p, q)\n        val right = lowestCommonAncestor(root.right, p, q)\n\n        return if (left != null && right != null) root else left ?: right\n\n    }\n}"  python="class LowestCommonAncestor {\n    def $1(root: TreeNode?, p: TreeNode?, q: TreeNode?): TreeNode? {\n        if (root == None || root === p || root === q) return root\n\n        $1 = lowestCommonAncestor(root.left, p, q)\n        $1 = lowestCommonAncestor(root.right, p, q)\n\n        return if (left != None && right != None) root else left ?: right\n\n    }\n}"  rust="class LowestCommonAncestor {\n    fn $1(root: TreeNode?, p: TreeNode?, q: TreeNode?): TreeNode? {\n        if (root == None || root === p || root === q) return root\n\n        val left = lowestCommonAncestor(root.left, p, q)\n        val right = lowestCommonAncestor(root.right, p, q)\n\n        return if (left != None && right != None) root else left ?: right\n\n    }\n}"  cpp="class LowestCommonAncestor {\n    $1(root: TreeNode?, p: TreeNode?, q: TreeNode?): TreeNode? {\n        if (root == nullptr || root === p || root === q) return root\n\n        auto $1 = lowestCommonAncestor(root.left, p, q)\n        auto $1 = lowestCommonAncestor(root.right, p, q)\n\n        return if (left != nullptr && right != nullptr) root else left ?: right\n\n    }\n}" %}

## LowestCommonAncestor_III

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/LowestCommonAncestor_III.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nclass LowestCommonAncestor_III {\n    class Node(var `val`: Int) {\n        var left: TreeNode? = null\n        var right: TreeNode? = null\n        var parent: Node? = null\n    }\n\n    fun lowestCommonAncestor(p: Node?, q: Node?): Node? {\n        var parent1 = p\n        var parent2 = q\n\n        while (parent1 != parent2) {\n            // Move parent1 upwards, or switch to q if it becomes null\n            parent1 = parent1?.parent ?: q\n            // Move parent2 upwards, or switch to p if it becomes null\n            parent2 = parent2?.parent ?: p\n        }\n\n        // parent1 and parent2 are now pointing to the same node, which is the LCA\n        return parent1\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n *       1 <- r\n *      / \\\n *     2   3\n *    /\\   /\\\n *   6 7   8 9 <-l\n *            \\\n *            10\n *\n */"  java="class LowestCommonAncestor_III {\n    class Node(var `val`) {\n        var left: TreeNode? = null\n        var right: TreeNode? = null\n        var parent: Node? = null\n    }\n\n    public static void $1(p: Node?, q: Node?): Node? {\n        var parent1 = p\n        var parent2 = q\n\n        while (parent1 != parent2) {\n            // Move parent1 upwards, or switch to q if it becomes null\n            parent1 = parent1?.parent ?: q\n            // Move parent2 upwards, or switch to p if it becomes null\n            parent2 = parent2?.parent ?: p\n        }\n\n        // parent1 and parent2 are now pointing to the same node, which is the LCA\n        return parent1\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n *       1 <- r\n *      / \\\n *     2   3\n *    /\\   /\\\n *   6 7   8 9 <-l\n *            \\\n *            10\n *\n */"  python="class LowestCommonAncestor_III {\n    class Node(var `val`: int) {\n        var left: TreeNode? = None\n        var right: TreeNode? = None\n        var parent: Node? = None\n    }\n\n    def $1(p: Node?, q: Node?): Node? {\n        $1 = p\n        $1 = q\n\n        while (parent1 != parent2) {\n            // Move parent1 upwards, or switch to q if it becomes None\n            parent1 = parent1?.parent ?: q\n            // Move parent2 upwards, or switch to p if it becomes None\n            parent2 = parent2?.parent ?: p\n        }\n\n        // parent1 and parent2 are now pointing to the same node, which is the LCA\n        return parent1\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n *       1 <- r\n *      / \\\n *     2   3\n *    /\\   /\\\n *   6 7   8 9 <-l\n *            \\\n *            10\n *\n */"  rust="class LowestCommonAncestor_III {\n    class Node(var `val` -> i32) {\n        var left: TreeNode? = None\n        var right: TreeNode? = None\n        var parent: Node? = None\n    }\n\n    fn $1(p: Node?, q: Node?): Node? {\n        var parent1 = p\n        var parent2 = q\n\n        while (parent1 != parent2) {\n            // Move parent1 upwards, or switch to q if it becomes None\n            parent1 = parent1?.parent ?: q\n            // Move parent2 upwards, or switch to p if it becomes None\n            parent2 = parent2?.parent ?: p\n        }\n\n        // parent1 and parent2 are now pointing to the same node, which is the LCA\n        return parent1\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n *       1 <- r\n *      / \\\n *     2   3\n *    /\\   /\\\n *   6 7   8 9 <-l\n *            \\\n *            10\n *\n */"  cpp="class LowestCommonAncestor_III {\n    class Node(var `val`) {\n        var left: TreeNode? ## MaximumSumBSTInBinaryTree

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nclass MaximumSumBSTInBinaryTree {\n    data class Result(val isBST: Boolean, val sum: Int, val min: Int, val max: Int)\n    private var maxSum = 0\n\n    fun maxSumBST(root: TreeNode?): Int {\n        dfs(root)\n        return maxSum\n    }\n\n    private fun dfs(node: TreeNode?): Result {\n        // Base case: if the node is null, it's node.`val` < right.min) {\n            // Current node is part of a valid BST\n            val sum = node.`val` + left.sum + right.sum\n            maxSum = maxOf(maxSum, sum) // Update the global max ## MaximumWidthOfBinaryTree

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/MaximumWidthOfBinaryTree.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nimport java.util.*\n\nclass MaximumWidthOfBinaryTree {\n    data class Node(var node: TreeNode?, var index: Int)\n\n    fun widthOfBinaryTree(root: TreeNode?): Int {\n        val queue: Queue<Node> = LinkedList<Node>()\n        var max = 0\n        queue.add(Node(root, 0))\n\n        while (queue.isNotEmpty()) {\n            var size = queue.size\n            var left = queue.peek().index\n            var right = left\n            repeat(size) {\n                val current = queue.poll()\n                right = current.index\n\n                current.node?.left?.let { queue.add(Node(it, 2 * current.index + 1)) }\n                current.node?.right?.let { queue.add(Node(it, 2 * current.index + 2)) }\n            }\n\n            max = maxOf(max, right - ## MinimumTimeToCollectAllApplesInATree

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/MinimumTimeToCollectAllApplesInATree.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nclass MinimumTimeToCollectAllApplesInATree {\n    fun minTime(n: Int, edges: Array<IntArray>, hasApple: List<Boolean>): Int {\n        // Build the graph as a list of lists (adjacency list representation)\n        val graph = Array(n) { mutableListOf<Int>() }\n        edges.forEach { (u, v) ->\n            graph[u].add(v)\n ## PathSum

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nclass PathSum {\n    fun hasPathSum(root: TreeNode?, targetSum: Int): Boolean {\n        return when {\n            root == null -> false\n            root.left == null && root.right == null && targetSum == root.`val` -> true\n            else -> hasPathSum(root.left, targetSum - root.`val`)\n                    || hasPathSum(root.right, targetSum - root.`val`)\n        }\n    }\n}"  java="class PathSum {\n    public static void $1(root: TreeNode?, targetSum) {\n        return when {\n            root == null -> false\n            root.left == null && root.right == null && targetSum == root.`val` -> true\n            else -> hasPathSum(root.left, targetSum - root.`val`)\n                    || hasPathSum(root.right, targetSum - root.`val`)\n        }\n    }\n}"  python="class PathSum {\n    def $1(root: TreeNode?, targetSum: int): bool {\n        return when {\n            root == None -> False\n            root.left == None && root.right == None && targetSum == root.`val` -> True\n            else -> hasPathSum(root.left, targetSum - root.`val`)\n                    || hasPathSum(root.right, targetSum - root.`val`)\n        }\n    }\n}"  rust="class PathSum {\n    fn $1(root: TreeNode?, targetSum -> i32) -> bool {\n        return when {\n            root == None -> false\n            root.left == None && root.right == None && targetSum == root.`val` -> true\n            else -> hasPathSum(root.left, targetSum - root.`val`)\n                    || hasPathSum(root.right, targetSum - root.`val`)\n        }\n    }\n}"  cpp="class PathSum {\n    $1(root: TreeNode?, targetSum) {\n        return when {\n            root == nullptr -> false\n            root.left == nullptr && root.right == nullptr && targetSum == root.`val` -> true\n            else -> hasPathSum(root.left, targetSum - root.`val`)\n                    || hasPathSum(root.right, targetSum - root.`val`)\n        }\n    }\n}" %}

## PathSumIII

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/PathSumIII.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nclass PathSumIII {\n    // O(N^2) solution\n    fun pathSum(root: TreeNode?, targetSum: Int): Int {\n        if (root == null)\n            return 0\n\n        // Count paths with targetSum starting from the current node\n        fun dfs(node: TreeNode?, currentSum: Long): Int {\n            if (node == null)\n                return 0\n\n            val newSum = currentSum + node.`val`\n            val count = if (newSum == targetSum.toLong()) 1 else 0\n\n            return count + dfs(node.left, newSum) + dfs(node.right, newSum)\n        }\n\n        // Start counting paths from the root\n        return dfs(root, 0L) + pathSum(root.left, targetSum) + pathSum(root.right, targetSum)\n    }\n\n\n    // Revisit I didn't understand\n    fun pathSum_prefix_sum(root: TreeNode?, targetSum: Int): Int {\n        // HashMap to store prefix sums and their frequencies\n        val prefixSumCount = HashMap<Long, Int>()\n        // Initialize with a prefix sum of 0 having occurred once (considering no node)\n        prefixSumCount[0L] = 1\n\n        // Helper function to perform DFS\n        fun dfs(node: TreeNode?, currentSum: Long): Int {\n            if (node == null) return 0\n\n            // Calculate the current sum at the current node\n            val newSum = currentSum + node.`val`\n\n            // Calculate how many valid paths end at the current node\n            var pathCount = prefixSumCount.getOrDefault(newSum - targetSum.toLong(), 0)\n\n            // Update prefix sum count\n            prefixSumCount[newSum] = prefixSumCount.getOrDefault(newSum, 0) + 1\n\n            // Recursively count paths in the left and right subtrees\n            pathCount += dfs(node.left, newSum)\n            pathCount += dfs(node.right, newSum)\n\n            // Backtrack: Remove the current prefix sum to avoid influencing other paths\n            prefixSumCount[newSum] = prefixSumCount.getOrDefault(newSum, 0) - 1\n\n            return pathCount\n        }\n\n        // Start DFS traversal from the root with initial current sum of 0\n        return dfs(root, 0L)\n    }\n}\n"  java="class PathSumIII {\n    // O(N^2) solution\n    public static void $1(root: TreeNode?, targetSum) {\n        if (root == null)\n            return 0\n\n        // Count paths with targetSum starting from the current node\n        public static void $1(node: TreeNode?, currentSum: Long) {\n            if (node == null)\n                return 0\n\n            val newSum = currentSum + node.`val`\n            val count = if (newSum == targetSum.toLong()) 1 else 0\n\n            return count + dfs(node.left, newSum) + dfs(node.right, newSum)\n        }\n\n        // Start counting paths from the root\n        return dfs(root, 0L) + pathSum(root.left, targetSum) + pathSum(root.right, targetSum)\n    }\n\n\n    // Revisit I didn't understand\n    public static void $1(root: TreeNode?, targetSum) {\n        // HashMap to store prefix sums and their frequencies\n        val prefixSumCount = HashMap<Long, Int>()\n        // Initialize with a prefix sum of 0 having occurred once (considering no node)\n        prefixSumCount[0L] = 1\n\n        // Helper function to perform DFS\n        public static void $1(node: TreeNode?, currentSum: Long) {\n            if (node == null) return 0\n\n            // Calculate the current sum at the current node\n            val newSum = currentSum + node.`val`\n\n            // Calculate how many valid paths end at the current node\n            var pathCount = prefixSumCount.getOrDefault(newSum - targetSum.toLong(), 0)\n\n            // Update prefix sum count\n            prefixSumCount[newSum] = prefixSumCount.getOrDefault(newSum, 0) + 1\n\n            // Recursively count paths in the left and right subtrees\n            pathCount += dfs(node.left, newSum)\n            pathCount += dfs(node.right, newSum)\n\n            // Backtrack: Remove the current prefix sum to avoid influencing other paths\n            prefixSumCount[newSum] = prefixSumCount.getOrDefault(newSum, 0) - ## PathSum_II

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/PathSum_II.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nclass PathSum_II {\n    fun pathSum(root: TreeNode?, targetSum: Int): List<List<Int>> {\n        val result = mutableListOf<List<Int>>()\n\n        fun dfs(node: TreeNode?, currentSum: Int, path: MutableList<Int> = mutableListOf()) {\n            if (node == null) return\n\n            // Add the current node's value to the path\n            path.add(node.`val`)\n\n            // If the node is a leaf and the path sum equals targetSum, add the path to the result\n            if (node.left == null && node.right == null && currentSum == node.`val`) {\n                result.add(path.toList()) // copy the current path list and add\n            } else {\n                // Continue the search on the left and right subtree\n                dfs(node.left, currentSum - node.`val`, path)\n                dfs(node.right, currentSum - node.`val`, path)\n            }\n\n            // Backtrack: remove the current node from the path\n            path.removeAt(path.size - 1)\n        }\n\n        dfs(root, targetSum)\n        return result\n    }\n}"  java="class PathSum_II {\n    public static void $1(root: TreeNode?, targetSum): List<List<Int>> {\n        val result = mutableListOf<List<Int>>()\n\n        public static void $1(node: TreeNode?, currentSum, path: MutableList<Int> = mutableListOf()) {\n            if (node == null) return\n\n            // Add the current node's value to the path\n            path.add(node.`val`)\n\n            // If the node is a leaf and the path sum equals targetSum, add the path to the result\n            if (node.left == null && node.right == null && currentSum == node.`val`) {\n                result.add(path.toList()) // copy the current path list and add\n            } else {\n                // Continue the search on the left and right subtree\n                dfs(node.left, currentSum - ## PopulateNextRightPointersInEachNode_II

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nimport java.util.*\n\nclass PopulateNextRightPointersInEachNode_II {\n    fun connect(root: Node?): Node? {\n        val queue: Queue<Node> = LinkedList()\n        root?.let { queue.add(it) }\n        while (queue.isNotEmpty()) {\n            var prev: Node? = null\n            repeat(queue.size) {\n                val node = queue.poll()\n                node?.left?.let { queue.add(it) }\n                node?.right?.let { queue.add(it) }\n\n                prev?.let{ prev?.next = node }\n                prev = node\n            }\n        }\n        return root\n    }\n}"  java="class PopulateNextRightPointersInEachNode_II {\n    public static void $1(root: Node?): Node? ## PopulateNextRightPointersInEachNode_II_Constant

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/PopulateNextRightPointersInEachNode_II_Constant.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nimport java.util.*\n\nclass PopulateNextRightPointersInEachNode_II_Constant {\n    fun connect(root: Node?): Node? {\n        var current: Node? = root\n\n        while (current != null) {\n            var nextLevelStart: Node? = null\n            var prev: Node? = null\n            var node = current\n\n            // Traverse the current level\n            while (node != null) {\n                // Connect left child\n                if (node.left != null) {\n                    if (prev != null) prev.next = node.left\n                    prev = node.left\n                    if (nextLevelStart == null) nextLevelStart = node.left\n                }\n\n                // Connect right child\n                if (node.right != null) {\n                    if (prev != null) prev.next = node.right\n                    prev = node.right\n                    if (nextLevelStart == null) nextLevelStart = node.right\n                }\n\n                node = node.next\n            }\n\n            // Move to the next level\n            current = nextLevelStart\n        }\n\n        return root\n    }\n}"  java="class PopulateNextRightPointersInEachNode_II_Constant {\n    public static void $1(root: Node?): Node? ## PopulatingNextRightPointerInEachNode

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nimport java.util.*\n\nclass Node(var `val`: Int) {\n    var left: Node? = null\n    var right: Node? = null\n    var next: Node? = null\n}\n\nclass PopulatingNextRightPointerInEachNode {\n    fun connect(root: Node?): Node? ## RecoverATreeFromPreOrderTraversal

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/RecoverATreeFromPreOrderTraversal.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nclass RecoverATreeFromPreOrderTraversal {\n    fun recoverFromPreorder(traversal: String): TreeNode? {\n        var index = 0 // Global index to track position in the string\n\n        // Recursive function to build the tree\n        fun buildTree(depth: Int): TreeNode? {\n            if (index >= traversal.length) return null // Base case: end of string\n\n            // Read the depth of the current node\n            var currentDepth = 0\n            while (index < traversal.length && traversal[index] == '-') {\n                currentDepth++\n                index++\n            }\n\n            // If the current depth doesn't match the expected depth, backtrack\n            if (currentDepth != depth) {\n                index -= currentDepth // Rewind the index\n                return null\n            }\n\n            // Read the value of the current node\n            var value = 0\n            while (index < traversal.length && traversal[index].isDigit()) {\n                value = value * 10 + (traversal[index] - '0')\n                index++\n            }\n\n            // Create the current node\n            val node = TreeNode(value)\n\n            // Recursively build the left and right subtrees\n            node.left = buildTree(depth + 1)\n            node.right = buildTree(depth + 1)\n\n            return node\n        }\n\n        return buildTree(0) // Start building the tree from depth 0\n    }\n}\n"  java="class RecoverATreeFromPreOrderTraversal {\n    public static void $1(traversal): TreeNode? ## SerializeAndDeserializeABinaryTree

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/SerializeAndDeserializeABinaryTree.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\n/**\n * Definition for a binary tree node.\n * class TreeNode(var `val`: Int) {\n *     var left: TreeNode? = null\n *     var right: TreeNode? = null\n * }\n */\n\nclass Codec() {\n    // Encodes a URL to a shortened URL.\n    fun serialize(root: TreeNode?): String {\n        val serializedTree = StringBuilder()\n\n        fun dfs(node: TreeNode?) {\n            if (node == null) {\n                serializedTree.append(\"null,\")\n                return\n            }\n\n            serializedTree.append(\"${node.`val`},\").also {\n                dfs(node.left)\n                dfs(node.right)\n            }\n        }\n        dfs(root)\n        return serializedTree.toString()\n    }\n\n    // Decodes the encoded string to tree using a recursive approach.\n    fun deserialize(data: String): TreeNode? {\n        val nodes = data.split(\",\").toMutableList()\n\n        fun dfsDeserialize(): TreeNode? {\n            if (nodes.isEmpty()) return null\n            val value = nodes.removeAt(0)\n            if (value == \"null\") return null\n\n            val node = TreeNode(value.toInt()).apply {\n                left = dfsDeserialize()\n                right = dfsDeserialize()\n            }\n\n            return node\n        }\n\n        return dfsDeserialize()\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Your Codec object will be instantiated and called as such:\n * var ser = Codec()\n * var deser = Codec()\n * var data = ser.serialize(longUrl)\n * var ans = deser.deserialize(data)\n */"  java="/**\n * Definition for a binary tree node.\n * class TreeNode(var `val`) {\n *     var left: TreeNode? ## SerializeAndDeserializeNArrayTree

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/SerializeAndDeserializeNArrayTree.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nclass SerializeAndDeserializeNArrayTree {\n    class Node(var `val`: Int) {\n        var children: List<Node?> = listOf()\n    }\n\n    class Codec {\n        // Encodes a tree to a single string.\n        fun serialize(root: Node?): String = when (root) {\n            null -> \"\"\n            else -> buildString {\n                fun dfs(node: Node?) {\n                    node?.let {\n                        append(\"${it.`val`}:${it.children.size}\")\n                        if (it.children.isNotEmpty()) append(\",\")\n                        it.children.forEachIndexed { index, child ->\n                            dfs(child)\n                            if (index < it.children.size - 1) append(\",\")\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n                dfs(root)\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Deserialize with internal DFS\n        fun deserialize(data: String): Node? {\n            if (data.isEmpty()) return null\n\n            val tokens = data.split(\",\")\n            var index = 0\n\n            fun parse(): Node? {\n                if (index >= tokens.size) return null\n\n                // Use destructuring declaration\n                val (valueStr, childCountStr) = tokens[index++].split(\":\")\n                val node = Node(valueStr.toInt())\n\n                // Create children using functional approach\n                node.children = List(childCountStr.toInt()) { parse() }\n\n                return node\n            }\n\n            return parse()\n        }\n    }\n}\n"  java="class SerializeAndDeserializeNArrayTree {\n    class Node(var `val`) {\n        var children: List<Node?> = listOf()\n    }\n\n    class Codec {\n        // Encodes a tree to a single string.\n        public static void $1(root: Node?) = when (root) {\n            null -> \"\"\n            else -> buildString {\n                public static void $1(node: Node?) {\n                    node?.let {\n                        append(\"${it.`val`}:${it.children.size}\")\n                        if (it.children.isNotEmpty()) append(\",\")\n                        it.children.forEachIndexed { index, child ->\n                            dfs(child)\n                            if (index < it.children.size - 1) append(\",\")\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n                dfs(root)\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Deserialize with internal DFS\n        public static void $1(data): Node? ## StepByStepDirectionsFromANodeToAnother

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/StepByStepDirectionsFromANodeToAnother.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nclass StepByStepDirectionsFromANodeToAnother {\n    fun findNode(root: TreeNode?, searchKey: Int): TreeNode? {\n        return when {\n            root == null -> null\n            root.`val` == searchKey -> root\n            else -> findNode(root.left, searchKey) ?: findNode(root.right, searchKey)\n        }\n    }\n\n    fun lowestCommonAncestor(root: TreeNode?, p: TreeNode?, q: TreeNode?): TreeNode? {\n        if (root == null || root === p || root === q) return root\n\n        val left = lowestCommonAncestor(root.left, p, q)\n        val right = lowestCommonAncestor(root.right, p, q)\n\n        return if (left != null && right != null) root else left ?: right\n\n    }\n\n    fun getDirections(root: TreeNode?, startValue: Int, destValue: Int): String {\n        val sourceNode = findNode(root, startValue)\n        val destNode = findNode(root, destValue)\n\n        if (sourceNode == null || destNode == null) {\n            return \"\" // No output for missing source or destination\n        }\n\n        val lca = lowestCommonAncestor(root, sourceNode, destNode)\n\n        val sourcePath = StringBuilder()\n        val destPath = StringBuilder()\n\n        buildPath(lca, sourceNode, sourcePath)\n        buildPath(lca, destNode, destPath)\n\n        val upMoves = \"U\".repeat(sourcePath.length)\n        return \"$upMoves${destPath.toString()}\"\n    }\n\n    private fun buildPath(node: TreeNode?, target: TreeNode?, path: StringBuilder): Boolean {\n        if (node == null) return false\n        if (node === target) return true\n\n        path.append('L')\n        if (buildPath(node.left, target, path)) return true\n        path.deleteCharAt(path.length - 1)\n\n        path.append('R')\n        if (buildPath(node.right, target, path)) return true\n        path.deleteCharAt(path.length - 1)\n\n        return false\n    }\n}\n"  java="class StepByStepDirectionsFromANodeToAnother {\n    public static void $1(root: TreeNode?, searchKey): TreeNode? {\n        return when {\n            root == null -> null\n            root.`val` == searchKey -> root\n            else -> findNode(root.left, searchKey) ?: findNode(root.right, searchKey)\n        }\n    }\n\n    public static void $1(root: TreeNode?, p: TreeNode?, q: TreeNode?): TreeNode? {\n        if (root == null || root === p || root === q) return root\n\n        val left = lowestCommonAncestor(root.left, p, q)\n        val right = lowestCommonAncestor(root.right, p, q)\n\n        return if (left != null && right != null) root else left ?: right\n\n    }\n\n    public static void $1(root: TreeNode?, startValue, destValue) {\n        val sourceNode = findNode(root, startValue)\n        val destNode = findNode(root, destValue)\n\n        if (sourceNode == null || destNode == null) {\n            return \"\" // No output for missing source or destination\n        }\n\n        val lca = lowestCommonAncestor(root, sourceNode, destNode)\n\n        val sourcePath = StringBuilder()\n        val destPath = StringBuilder()\n\n        buildPath(lca, sourceNode, sourcePath)\n        buildPath(lca, destNode, destPath)\n\n        val upMoves = \"U\".repeat(sourcePath.length)\n        return \"$upMoves${destPath.toString()}\"\n    }\n\n    private public static void $1(node: TreeNode?, target: TreeNode?, path: StringBuilder) {\n        if (node == null) return false\n        if (node === target) return true\n\n        path.append('L')\n        if (buildPath(node.left, target, path)) return true\n        path.deleteCharAt(path.length - 1)\n\n        path.append('R')\n        if (buildPath(node.right, target, path)) return true\n        path.deleteCharAt(path.length - 1)\n\n        return false\n    }\n}"  python="class StepByStepDirectionsFromANodeToAnother {\n    def $1(root: TreeNode?, searchKey: int): TreeNode? {\n        return when {\n            root == None -> None\n            root.`val` == searchKey -> root\n            else -> findNode(root.left, searchKey) ?: findNode(root.right, searchKey)\n        }\n    }\n\n    def $1(root: TreeNode?, p: TreeNode?, q: TreeNode?): TreeNode? {\n        if (root == None || root === p || root === q) return root\n\n        $1 = lowestCommonAncestor(root.left, p, q)\n        $1 = lowestCommonAncestor(root.right, p, q)\n\n        return if (left != None && right != None) root else left ?: right\n\n    }\n\n    def $1(root: TreeNode?, startValue: int, destValue: int): str {\n        $1 = findNode(root, startValue)\n        $1 = findNode(root, destValue)\n\n        if (sourceNode == None || destNode == None) {\n            return \"\" // No output for missing source or destination\n        }\n\n        $1 = lowestCommonAncestor(root, sourceNode, destNode)\n\n        $1 = StringBuilder()\n        $1 = StringBuilder()\n\n        buildPath(lca, sourceNode, sourcePath)\n        buildPath(lca, destNode, destPath)\n\n        $1 = \"U\".repeat(sourcePath.length)\n        return \"$upMoves${destPath.toString()}\"\n    }\n\n    private def $1(node: TreeNode?, target: TreeNode?, path: StringBuilder): bool {\n        if (node == None) return False\n        if (node === target) return True\n\n        path.append('L')\n        if (buildPath(node.left, target, path)) return True\n        path.deleteCharAt(path.length - 1)\n\n        path.append('R')\n        if (buildPath(node.right, target, path)) return True\n        path.deleteCharAt(path.length - 1)\n\n        return False\n    }\n}"  rust="class StepByStepDirectionsFromANodeToAnother {\n    fn $1(root: TreeNode?, searchKey -> i32): TreeNode? ## VerticalOrderTraversalOfABinaryTree

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/VerticalOrderTraversalOfABinaryTree.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree\n\nimport java.util.*\n\nclass VerticalOrderTraversalOfABinaryTree {\n    data class VerticalIndex(val node: TreeNode, val verticalIndex: Int)\n\n    fun verticalTraversal(root: TreeNode?): List<List<Int>> {\n        if (root == null) return emptyList()\n\n        val columnTable = mutableMapOf<Int, TreeSet<Int>>()\n        var minColumn = 0\n        var maxColumn = 0\n\n        val queue: Queue<VerticalIndex> = LinkedList()\n        queue.offer(VerticalIndex(root, 0))\n\n        while (queue.isNotEmpty()) {\n            val (node, column) = queue.poll()\n\n            columnTable.getOrPut(column) { TreeSet() }.add(node.`val`)\n\n            // Update min and max column indices\n            minColumn = minOf(minColumn, column)\n            maxColumn = maxOf(maxColumn, column)\n\n            node.left?.let { queue.offer(VerticalIndex(it, column - 1)) }\n            node.right?.let { queue.offer(VerticalIndex(it, column + 1)) }\n        }\n\n        val result = mutableListOf<List<Int>>()\n        for (col in minColumn..maxColumn) {\n            result.add(columnTable[col]!!.toList())\n        }\n\n        return result\n    }\n}"  java="class VerticalOrderTraversalOfABinaryTree {\n    data class VerticalIndex(val node: TreeNode, val verticalIndex)\n\n    public static void $1(root: TreeNode?): List<List<Int>> {\n        if (root == null) return emptyList()\n\n        val columnTable = mutableMapOf<Int, TreeSet<Int>>()\n        var minColumn = 0\n        var maxColumn = 0\n\n        val queue: Queue<VerticalIndex> = LinkedList()\n        queue.offer(VerticalIndex(root, 0))\n\n        while (queue.isNotEmpty()) {\n            val (node, column) = queue.poll()\n\n            columnTable.getOrPut(column) { TreeSet() }.add(node.`val`)\n\n            // Update min and max column indices\n            minColumn = minOf(minColumn, column)\n            maxColumn = maxOf(maxColumn, column)\n\n            node.left?.let { queue.offer(VerticalIndex(it, column - ## MinCostToConnectAllPointsKruskal

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/mst/MinCostToConnectAllPointsKruskal.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree.mst\n\nimport kotlin.math.abs\n\nclass MinCostToConnectAllPointsKruskal {\n    data class Edge(val point1: Int, val point2: Int, val weight: Int)\n\n    data class UnionFindNode(var parent: Int, var rank: Int)\n\n    val manhattanDistance = { p1: IntArray, p2: IntArray -> abs(p1[0] - p2[0]) + abs(p1[1] - p2[1]) }\n\n    class UnionFind(size: Int) {\n        private val nodes = Array(size) { UnionFindNode(it, 0) }\n\n        fun find(x: Int): Int {\n            if (nodes[x].parent != x) {\n                nodes[x].parent = find(nodes[x].parent)\n            }\n            return nodes[x].parent\n        }\n\n        fun union(x: Int, y: Int) {\n            val rootX = find(x)\n            val rootY = find(y)\n            if (rootX != rootY) {\n                when {\n                    nodes[rootX].rank > nodes[rootY].rank -> nodes[rootY].parent = rootX\n                    nodes[rootX].rank < nodes[rootY].rank -> nodes[rootX].parent = rootY\n                    else -> {\n                        nodes[rootY].parent = rootX\n                        nodes[rootX].rank += 1\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    fun minCostConnectPoints(points: Array<IntArray>): Int {\n        val edges = mutableListOf<Edge>()\n        for (i in points.indices) {\n            for (j in i + 1 until points.size) {\n                edges.add(Edge(i, j, manhattanDistance(points[i], points[j])))\n            }\n        }\n        edges.sortBy { it.weight }\n\n        val uf = UnionFind(points.size)\n        var cost = 0\n        for (edge in edges) {\n            if (uf.find(edge.point1) != uf.find(edge.point2)) {\n                uf.union(edge.point1, edge.point2)\n                cost += edge.weight\n            }\n        }\n        return cost\n    }\n}\n"  java="class MinCostToConnectAllPointsKruskal {\n    data class Edge(val point1, val point2, val weight)\n\n    data class UnionFindNode(var parent, var rank)\n\n    val manhattanDistance = { p1: IntArray, p2: IntArray -> abs(p1[0] - p2[0]) + abs(p1[1] - p2[1]) }\n\n    class UnionFind(size) {\n        private val nodes = Array(size) { UnionFindNode(it, 0) }\n\n        public static void $1(x) {\n            if (nodes[x].parent != x) {\n                nodes[x].parent = find(nodes[x].parent)\n            }\n            return nodes[x].parent\n        }\n\n        public static void $1(x, y) {\n            val rootX = find(x)\n            val rootY = find(y)\n            if (rootX != rootY) {\n                when {\n                    nodes[rootX].rank > nodes[rootY].rank -> nodes[rootY].parent = rootX\n                    nodes[rootX].rank < nodes[rootY].rank -> nodes[rootX].parent = rootY\n                    else -> {\n                        nodes[rootY].parent = rootX\n                        nodes[rootX].rank += 1\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    public static void $1(points: Array<IntArray>) {\n        val edges = mutableListOf<Edge>()\n        for (i in points.indices) {\n            for (j in i + 1 until points.size) {\n                edges.add(Edge(i, j, manhattanDistance(points[i], points[j])))\n            }\n        }\n        edges.sortBy { it.weight }\n\n        val uf = UnionFind(points.size)\n        var cost = 0\n        for (edge in edges) {\n            if (uf.find(edge.point1) != uf.find(edge.point2)) {\n                uf.union(edge.point1, edge.point2)\n                cost += edge.weight\n            }\n        }\n        return cost\n    }\n}"  python="class MinCostToConnectAllPointsKruskal {\n    data class Edge(val point1: int, val point2: int, val weight: int)\n\n    data class UnionFindNode(var parent: int, var rank: int)\n\n    $1 = { p1: list[int], p2: list[int] -> abs(p1[0] - ## MinCostToConnectAllPointsPrims

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/mst/MinCostToConnectAllPointsPrims.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree.mst\n\nimport java.util.*\nimport kotlin.math.abs\n\n// Better for Dense Graph\nclass MinCostToConnectAllPointsPrims {\n    data class Node(val dest: Int, val weight: Int)\n    fun minCostConnectPoints(points: Array<IntArray>): Int {\n        fun dist(from: Int, to: Int) =\n            abs(points[from][0] - points[to][0]) + abs(points[from][1] - points[to][1])\n\n        val notVisited = points.indices.toMutableSet()\n        val pq = PriorityQueue<Node>(compareBy{ it.weight })\n        pq.add(Node(0, 0))\n        var totalCost = 0\n        while (notVisited.isNotEmpty()) {\n            val ( dest, weight ) = pq.poll()\n            if (!notVisited.remove(dest)) continue\n            totalCost += weight\n            for (neighbour in notVisited) pq.add(Node(neighbour , dist(dest, neighbour)))\n        }\n        return totalCost\n    }\n}\n"  java="// Better for Dense Graph\nclass MinCostToConnectAllPointsPrims {\n    data class Node(val dest, val weight)\n    public static void $1(points: Array<IntArray>) {\n        public static void $1(from, to) =\n            abs(points[from][0] - points[to][0]) + abs(points[from][1] - points[to][1])\n\n        val notVisited = points.indices.toMutableSet()\n        val pq = PriorityQueue<Node>(compareBy{ it.weight })\n        pq.add(Node(0, 0))\n        var totalCost = 0\n        while (notVisited.isNotEmpty()) {\n            val ( dest, weight ) = pq.poll()\n            if (!notVisited.remove(dest)) continue\n            totalCost += weight\n            for (neighbour in notVisited) pq.add(Node(neighbour , dist(dest, neighbour)))\n        }\n        return totalCost\n    }\n}"  python="// Better for Dense Graph\nclass MinCostToConnectAllPointsPrims {\n    data class Node(val dest: int, val weight: int)\n    def $1(points: Array<list[int]>): int {\n        def $1(from: int, to: int) =\n            abs(points[from][0] - {% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree.bfs\n\nimport tree.TreeNode\n\nclass CheckCompletenessOfBinaryTree {\n    fun isCompleteTree(root: TreeNode?): Boolean {\n        if (root == null) ## CountOfSmallerNumberAfterSelf

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/fenwick/CountOfSmallerNumberAfterSelf.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree.fenwick\n\nclass CountOfSmallerNumberAfterSelf {\n    fun countSmaller(nums: IntArray): List<Int> {\n        if (nums.isEmpty()) return emptyList()\n\n        // Step 1: Coordinate compression\n        val sorted = nums.toTypedArray().sorted()\n        val rankMap = HashMap<Int, Int>()\n        var rank = 1\n        for (num in sorted) {\n            if (num !in rankMap) {\n                rankMap[num] = rank++\n            }\n        }\n\n        val bit = FenwickTree(rank)\n        val res = IntArray(nums.size)\n\n        // Step 2: Traverse from right to left\n        for (i in nums.lastIndex downTo 0) {\n            val r = rankMap[nums[i]]!!\n            res[i] = bit.query(r - 1) // count of smaller numbers\n            bit.update(r, 1)          // add current number\n        }\n\n        return res.toList()\n    }\n\n    class FenwickTree(size: Int) {\n        private val tree = IntArray(size + 2)\n\n        fun update(index: Int, value: Int) {\n            var i = index\n            while (i < tree.size) {\n                tree[i] += value\n                i += i and -i\n            }\n        }\n\n        fun query(index: Int): Int {\n            var sum = 0\n            var i = index\n            while (i > 0) {\n                sum += tree[i]\n                i -= i and -i\n            }\n            return sum\n        }\n    }\n}\n"  java="class CountOfSmallerNumberAfterSelf {\n    public static void $1(nums: IntArray): List<Int> {\n        if (nums.isEmpty()) return emptyList()\n\n        // Step 1: Coordinate compression\n        val sorted = nums.toTypedArray().sorted()\n        val rankMap = HashMap<Int, Int>()\n        var rank = 1\n        for (num in sorted) {\n            if (num !in rankMap) {\n                rankMap[num] = rank++\n            }\n        }\n\n        val bit = FenwickTree(rank)\n        val res = IntArray(nums.size)\n\n        // Step 2: Traverse from right to left\n        for (i in nums.lastIndex downTo 0) {\n            val r = rankMap[nums[i]]!!\n            res[i] = bit.query(r - 1) // count of smaller numbers\n            bit.update(r, 1)          // add current number\n        }\n\n        return res.toList()\n    }\n\n    class FenwickTree(size) {\n        private val tree = IntArray(size + 2)\n\n        public static void $1(index, value) {\n            var i = index\n            while (i < tree.size) {\n                tree[i] += value\n                i += i and -i\n            }\n        }\n\n        public static void $1(index) {\n            var sum = 0\n            var i = index\n            while (i > 0) {\n                sum += tree[i]\n                i -= i and -i\n            }\n            return sum\n        }\n    }\n}"  python="class CountOfSmallerNumberAfterSelf {\n    def $1(nums: list[int]): List<Int> {\n        if (nums.isEmpty()) return emptyList()\n\n        // Step 1: Coordinate compression\n        $1 = nums.toTypedArray().sorted()\n        $1 = HashMap<Int, Int>()\n        $1 = 1\n        for (num in sorted) {\n            if (num !in rankMap) {\n                rankMap[num] = rank++\n            }\n        }\n\n        $1 = FenwickTree(rank)\n        $1 = list[int](nums.size)\n\n        // Step 2: Traverse from right to left\n        for (i in nums.lastIndex downTo 0) {\n            $1 = rankMap[nums[i]]!!\n            res[i] = bit.query(r - ## FenwickTree

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/fenwick/FenwickTree.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree.fenwick\n\nclass FenwickTree(size: Int) {\n    private val tree = IntArray(size + 1)\n\n    fun update(index: Int, value: Int) {\n        var i = index + 1\n        while (i < tree.size) {\n            tree[i] += value\n            i += i and -i\n        }\n    }\n\n    fun prefixSum(index: Int): Int {\n        var i = index + 1\n        var sum = 0\n        while (i > 0) {\n            sum += tree[i]\n            i -= i and -i\n        }\n        return sum\n    }\n\n    fun rangeSum(left: Int, right: Int): Int = prefixSum(right) - {% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree.bst\n\nclass BSTIterator(root: TreeNode?) {\n    private val stack = ArrayDeque<TreeNode>()\n\n    init {\n        // Initialize the stack by adding all ## ClosestBinarySearchTreeValue

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree.bst\n\nimport kotlin.math.abs\n\nclass ClosestBinarySearchTreeValue {\n    fun closestValue(root: TreeNode?, target: Double): Int {\n        var closest = root?.`val` ?: 0\n        var current = root\n\n        while (current != null) {\n            val currentValue = current.`val`\n\n            // Update closest based on the given conditions:\n            if (abs(currentValue - target) < abs(closest - target) ||\n                (abs(currentValue - target) == abs(closest - target) && currentValue < closest))\n                closest = currentValue\n\n            // Move to the left or right subtree based on the target\n            current = if (target < currentValue) current.left else current.right\n        }\n\n        return closest\n    }\n}"  java="class ClosestBinarySearchTreeValue {\n    public static void $1(root: TreeNode?, target: Double) {\n        var closest = root?.`val` ?: 0\n        var current = root\n\n        while (current != null) {\n            val currentValue = current.`val`\n\n            // Update closest based on the given conditions:\n            if (abs(currentValue - ## ConvertBInarySearchTreeToSortedDoublyLinkedList

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/bst/ConvertBInarySearchTreeToSortedDoublyLinkedList.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree.bst\n/**\n * Definition for a Node.\n class Node(var `val`: Int) {\n    var left: Node? = null\n    var right: Node? = null\n }\n */\nclass ConvertBInarySearchTreeToSortedDoublyLinkedList {\n    class Node(var `val`: Int) {\n        var left: Node? = null\n        var right: Node? = null\n    }\n\n    private var head: Node? = null\n    private var tail: Node? = null\n\n    fun treeToDoublyList(root: Node?): Node? {\n        if (root == null) return null\n\n        // Perform in-order traversal and link nodes\n        inorderTraversal(root)\n\n        // Complete the doubly linked list by linking head and tail\n        head?.left = tail\n        tail?.right = head\n\n        return head\n    }\n\n    private fun inorderTraversal(node: Node?) {\n        if (node == null) return\n\n        inorderTraversal(node.left) // Traverse left subtree\n\n        if (tail != null) {\n            // Link the current node with the previous node (tail)\n            tail!!.right = node\n            node.left = tail\n        } else {\n            // This is the first node (head of the doubly linked list)\n            head = node\n        }\n\n        // Update the tail to the current node\n        tail = node\n\n        inorderTraversal(node.right) // Traverse right subtree\n    }\n}"  java="/**\n * Definition for a Node.\n class Node(var `val`) {\n    var left: Node? = null\n    var right: Node? = null\n }\n */\nclass ConvertBInarySearchTreeToSortedDoublyLinkedList {\n    class Node(var `val`) {\n        var left: Node? = null\n        var right: Node? = null\n    }\n\n    private var head: Node? = null\n    private var tail: Node? = null\n\n    public static void $1(root: Node?): Node? {\n        if (root == null) return null\n\n        // Perform in-order traversal and link nodes\n        inorderTraversal(root)\n\n        // Complete the doubly linked list by linking head and tail\n        head?.left = tail\n        tail?.right = head\n\n        return head\n    }\n\n    private public static void $1(node: Node?) {\n        if (node == null) return\n\n        inorderTraversal(node.left) // Traverse left subtree\n\n        if (tail != null) {\n            // Link the current node with the previous node (tail)\n            tail!!.right = node\n            node.left = tail\n        } else {\n            // This is the first node (head of the doubly linked list)\n            head = node\n        }\n\n        // Update the tail to the current node\n        tail = node\n\n        inorderTraversal(node.right) // Traverse right subtree\n    }\n}"  python="/**\n * Definition for a Node.\n class Node(var `val`: int) {\n    var left: Node? = None\n    private var tail: Node? = None\n\n    def $1(root: Node?): Node? {\n        if (root == None) return None\n\n        // Perform in-order traversal and link nodes\n        inorderTraversal(root)\n\n        // Complete the doubly linked list by linking head and tail\n        head?.left = tail\n        tail?.right = head\n\n        return head\n    }\n\n    private def $1(node: Node?) {\n        if (node == None) return\n\n        inorderTraversal(node.left) // Traverse left subtree\n\n        if (tail != None) {\n            // Link the current node with the previous node (tail)\n            tail!!.right = node\n            node.left = tail\n        } else {\n            // This is the first node (head of the doubly linked list)\n            head = node\n        }\n\n        // Update the tail to the current node\n        tail = node\n\n        inorderTraversal(node.right) // Traverse right subtree\n    }\n}"  rust="/**\n * Definition for a Node.\n class Node(var `val` -> i32) {\n    var left: Node? ## DeleteNodeinABST

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/bst/DeleteNodeinABST.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree.bst\n\nclass TreeNode(var `val`: Int) {\n    var left: TreeNode? = null\n    var right: TreeNode? = null\n}\n\nclass DeleteNodeinABST {\n    fun deleteNode(root: TreeNode?, key: Int): TreeNode? {\n        when {\n            root == null -> return null\n            key < root.`val` -> root.left = deleteNode(root.left, key)\n            key > root.`val` -> root.right = deleteNode(root.right, key)\n            else -> {\n                when {\n                    root.left == null -> return root.right\n                    root.right == null -> return root.left\n                    else -> {\n                        root.`val` = minValue(root.right!!)\n                        root.right = deleteNode(root.right, root.`val`)\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        return root\n    }\n\n    fun minValue(node: TreeNode): Int {\n        var current = node\n        while (current.left != null) {\n            current = current.left!!\n        }\n\n        return current.`val`\n    }\n}"  java="class TreeNode(var `val`) {\n    var left: TreeNode? ## InorderSuccessor

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/bst/InorderSuccessor.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree.bst\n\nclass InorderSuccessor {\n    fun inorderSuccessor(root: TreeNode?, p: TreeNode?): TreeNode? {\n        var successor: TreeNode? = null\n        var current = root\n\n        while (current != null) {\n            if (p!!.`val` < current.`val`) {\n                // If p's value is less than current, the successor is possibly current\n                successor = current\n                current = current.left\n            } else {\n                // If p's value is greater or equal to current, move to the right subtree\n                current = current.right\n            }\n        }\n\n        return successor\n    }\n}"  java="class InorderSuccessor {\n    public static void $1(root: TreeNode?, p: TreeNode?): TreeNode? ## LongestIncreasingSubsequence

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/bst/LongestIncreasingSubsequence.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree.bst\n\nimport java.util.*\n\n// Patience sorting algorithm\nclass LongestIncreasingSubsequence {\n    fun lengthOfLIS(nums: IntArray): Int {\n        val tree = TreeSet<Int>()\n        nums.forEach { num ->\n            // Find the smallest element in the tree which is greater than or equal to num\n            tree.ceiling(num)?.also {\n                // If such an element is found, it means num can replace it to potentially\n                // form a new valid increasing subsequence or extend the current one\n                tree.remove(it)\n            }\n            // Add num to the tree. If num is not replacing any element,\n            // it is extending the subsequence with a new larger element.\n            tree.add(num)\n        }\n        // The size of the tree at the end will represent the length of the longest\n        // increasing subsequence\n        return tree.size\n    }\n}\n"  java="// Patience sorting algorithm\nclass LongestIncreasingSubsequence {\n    public static void $1(nums: IntArray) {\n        val tree = TreeSet<Int>()\n        nums.forEach { num ->\n            // Find the smallest element in the tree which is greater than or equal to num\n            tree.ceiling(num)?.also {\n                // If such an element is found, it means num can replace it to potentially\n                // form a new valid increasing subsequence or extend the current one\n                tree.remove(it)\n            }\n            // Add num to the tree. ## RecoverBinarySearchTree

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/tree/bst/RecoverBinarySearchTree.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree.bst\n\nclass RecoverBinarySearchTree {\n    fun recoverTree(root: TreeNode?) {\n        var first: TreeNode? = null\n        var second: TreeNode? = null\n        var prev: TreeNode? = null\n\n        // Helper function to perform in-order traversal\n        fun dfs(node: TreeNode?) {\n            if (node == null) return\n\n            // Traverse left subtree\n            dfs(node.left)\n\n            // Identify swapped nodes\n            if (prev != null && prev!!.`val` > node.`val`) {\n                if (first == null) {\n                    first = prev  // First out-of-order node\n                }\n                second = node  // Second out-of-order node\n            }\n\n            // Update previous node\n            prev = node\n\n            // Traverse right subtree\n            dfs(node.right)\n        }\n\n        // Step 1: In-order traversal to find the swapped nodes\n        dfs(root)\n\n        // Step 2: Swap the values of the two nodes\n        first?.let { f ->\n            second?.let { s ->\n                val temp = f.`val`\n                f.`val` = s.`val`\n                s.`val` = temp\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}"  java="class RecoverBinarySearchTree {\n    public static void $1(root: TreeNode?) {\n        var first: TreeNode? {% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package tree.bst\n\nimport java.util.*\n\nclass SkylineProblem {\n    fun getSkyline(buildings: Array<IntArray>): List<List<Int>> {\n        val points =
