## AutoCompleteSystem

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/trie/AutoCompleteSystem.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package trie\n\nimport java.util.*\n\nclass AutoCompleteTrie {\n    data class TrieNode(\n        var ch: Char='*',\n        var hotness: Int = 0,\n        var isSentence: Boolean = false,\n        var children: TreeMap<Char, TrieNode> = TreeMap()\n    )\n    data class SearchResultItem(var data: String, val hotness: Int)\n\n    val root = TrieNode()\n\n    fun append(word: String, hotness: Int = 1) {\n        var currentNode = root\n\n        word.forEach { ch->\n            currentNode = currentNode.children.getOrPut(ch){ TrieNode(ch) }\n        }\n\n        currentNode.isSentence = true\n        currentNode.hotness += hotness\n    }\n\n    fun rank(word: String, limit: Int = 3): List<String> {\n        val results = mutableListOf<SearchResultItem>()\n        var currentNode = root\n\n        word.forEach { ch -> currentNode = currentNode.children[ch] ?: return results.map{ it.data } }\n        // If we reach here, currentNode represents the node ending at 'word'\n        // Collect all words from this node downwards\n        collectWords(currentNode, word, results)\n\n\n        return results\n            .sortedByDescending { it.hotness } // Sort by hotness descending\n            .take(3) // Take the top 3 results\n            .map { it.data } // Extract only the data (sentences) from SearchResultItem\n    }\n\n    fun collectWords(node: TrieNode?, prefix: String, results: MutableList<SearchResultItem>) {\n        if (node == null)\n            return\n        if (node.isSentence)\n            results.add(SearchResultItem(data=prefix, hotness = node.hotness))\n\n        for((ch, childNode) in node.children) {\n            collectWords(childNode, prefix + ch, results)\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nclass AutocompleteSystem(sentences: Array<String>, times: IntArray) {\n    var prefix = StringBuilder()\n    var trie = AutoCompleteTrie()\n\n    init {\n        sentences.forEachIndexed{ index, word-> trie.append(word, times[index] ) }\n    }\n\n    fun input(c: Char): List<String> {\n\n        // If it's a # then time to end the character stream and insert all the buffered characters\n        // Also since the sentence is types again, increase it's hotness in the Trie data structure\n        if (c == '#') {\n            val sentence = prefix.toString()\n            trie.append(sentence)\n\n            prefix = StringBuilder()\n            return emptyList()\n        }\n\n        prefix.append(c)\n        return trie.rank(prefix.toString())\n    }\n}\n"  java="class AutoCompleteTrie {\n    data class TrieNode(\n        var ch: Char='*',\n        var hotness = 0,\n        var isSentence = false,\n        var children: TreeMap<Char, TrieNode> = TreeMap()\n    )\n    data class SearchResultItem(var data, val hotness)\n\n    val root = TrieNode()\n\n    public static void $1(word, hotness = 1) {\n        var currentNode = root\n\n        word.forEach { ch->\n            currentNode = currentNode.children.getOrPut(ch){ TrieNode(ch) }\n        }\n\n        currentNode.isSentence = true\n        currentNode.hotness += hotness\n    }\n\n    public static void $1(word, limit = 3): List<String> {\n        val results = mutableListOf<SearchResultItem>()\n        var currentNode = root\n\n        word.forEach { ch -> currentNode = currentNode.children[ch] ?: return results.map{ it.data } }\n        // If we reach here, currentNode represents the node ending at 'word'\n        // Collect all words from this node downwards\n        collectWords(currentNode, word, results)\n\n\n        return results\n            .sortedByDescending { it.hotness } // Sort by hotness descending\n            .take(3) // Take the top 3 results\n            .map { it.data } // Extract only the data (sentences) from SearchResultItem\n    }\n\n    public static void $1(node: TrieNode?, prefix, results: MutableList<SearchResultItem>) {\n        if (node == null)\n            return\n        if (node.isSentence)\n            results.add(SearchResultItem(data=prefix, hotness = node.hotness))\n\n ## AutoCompleteSystemWithHeap

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package trie\n\nclass AutoCompleteSystemWithHeap(sentences: Array<String>, times: IntArray) {\n    inner class TrieNode {\n        val children = Array<TrieNode?>(26) { null }\n        val suggestions = mutableListOf<String>()\n    }\n\n    val root = TrieNode()\n\n    init {\n        sentences.forEachIndexed { index, word ->\n            insert(word, times[index])\n        }\n    }\n\n    fun insert(word: String, hotness: Int) {\n        var currentNode = root\n\n        word.forEach { ch ->\n            val index = ch - 'a'\n            if (currentNode.children[index] == null) {\n                currentNode.children[index] = TrieNode()\n            }\n            currentNode = currentNode.children[index]!!\n            if (currentNode.suggestions.size < 3) {\n                currentNode.suggestions.add(word)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    fun search(prefix: String): List<String> {\n        var currentNode = root\n        val result = mutableListOf<String>()\n\n        prefix.forEach { ch ->\n            val index = ch - 'a'\n            if (currentNode.children[index] == null) {\n                return result\n            }\n            currentNode = currentNode.children[index]!!\n        }\n\n        // If we reach here, currentNode is the node representing the end of the prefix\n        return currentNode.suggestions.take(3)\n    }\n\n    fun suggestedProducts(searchWord: String): List<List<String>> {\n        val result = mutableListOf<List<String>>()\n        val prefixSearchString = StringBuilder()\n\n        searchWord.forEach { ch ->\n            prefixSearchString.append(ch)\n            result.add(search(prefixSearchString.toString()))\n        }\n\n        return result\n    }\n}"  java="class AutoCompleteSystemWithHeap(sentences: Array<String>, times: IntArray) {\n    inner class TrieNode {\n        val children = Array<TrieNode?>(26) { null }\n        val suggestions = mutableListOf<String>()\n    }\n\n    val root = TrieNode()\n\n    init {\n        sentences.forEachIndexed { index, word ->\n            insert(word, times[index])\n        }\n    }\n\n    public static void $1(word, hotness) {\n        var currentNode = root\n\n        word.forEach { ch ->\n            val index = ch - ## CountWordsWithAGivenPrefix_Trie

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/trie/CountWordsWithAGivenPrefix_Trie.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package trie\n\nclass CountWordsWithAGivenPrefix_Trie {\n    data class TrieNode(\n        val ch: Char = '_',\n        val children: MutableMap<Char, TrieNode> = mutableMapOf(),\n        var prefixCount: Int = 0\n    )\n\n    var root = TrieNode()\n\n    // Method to count the words with the given prefix\n    fun prefixCount(words: Array<String>, prefix: String): Int {\n        // Build the trie using the words\n        buildTrie(words, root)\n\n        // Traverse the trie to find the node corresponding to the given prefix\n        return findPrefixNode(prefix)?.prefixCount ?: 0\n    }\n\n    // Method to build the trie\n    private fun buildTrie(words: Array<String>, root: TrieNode) {\n        for (word in words) {\n            var current = root\n            for (ch in word) {\n                // Move to the child node or create a new one\n                current = current.children.getOrPut(ch) { TrieNode(ch) }\n                current.prefixCount++  // Increment prefix count for every node along the way\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Method to find the node corresponding to the last character of the prefix\n    private fun findPrefixNode(prefix: String): TrieNode? {\n        var current = root\n        for (ch in prefix) {\n            current = current.children[ch] ?: return null  // If prefix doesn't exist, return null\n        }\n        return current\n    }\n}\n"  java="class CountWordsWithAGivenPrefix_Trie {\n    data class TrieNode(\n        val ch: Char = '_',\n        val children: MutableMap<Char, TrieNode> = mutableMapOf(),\n        var prefixCount = 0\n    )\n\n    var root = TrieNode()\n\n    // Method to count the words with the given prefix\n    public static void $1(words: Array<String>, prefix) {\n        // Build the trie using the words\n        buildTrie(words, root)\n\n        // Traverse the trie to find the node corresponding to the given prefix\n        return findPrefixNode(prefix)?.prefixCount ?: 0\n    }\n\n    // Method to build the trie\n    private public static void $1(words: Array<String>, root: TrieNode) {\n        for (word in words) {\n            var current = root\n            for (ch in word) {\n                // Move to the child node or create a new one\n                current = current.children.getOrPut(ch) { TrieNode(ch) }\n                current.prefixCount++  // Increment prefix count for every node along the way\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Method to find the node corresponding to the last character of the prefix\n    private public static void $1(prefix): TrieNode? {\n        var current = root\n        for (ch in prefix) {\n            current = current.children[ch] ?: return null  // If prefix doesn't exist, return null\n        }\n        return current\n    }\n}"  python="class CountWordsWithAGivenPrefix_Trie {\n    data class TrieNode(\n        val ch: Char = '_',\n        val children: MutableMap<Char, TrieNode> = mutableMapOf(),\n        var prefixCount: int = 0\n    )\n\n    $1 = TrieNode()\n\n    // Method to count the words with the given prefix\n    def $1(words: Array<String>, prefix: str): int {\n        // Build the trie using the words\n        buildTrie(words, root)\n\n        // Traverse the trie to find the node corresponding to the given prefix\n        return findPrefixNode(prefix)?.prefixCount ?: 0\n    }\n\n    // Method to build the trie\n    private def $1(words: Array<String>, root: TrieNode) {\n        for (word in words) {\n            $1 = root\n            for (ch in word) {\n                // Move to the child node or create a new one\n                current = current.children.getOrPut(ch) { TrieNode(ch) }\n                current.prefixCount++  // Increment prefix count for every node along the way\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Method to find the node corresponding to the last character of the prefix\n    private def $1(prefix: str): TrieNode? ## CountWordsWithAGivenPrefix_Trie_FP

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/trie/CountWordsWithAGivenPrefix_Trie_FP.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package trie\n\nclass CountWordsWithAGivenPrefix_Trie_FP {\n    data class TrieNode(val children: MutableMap<Char, TrieNode> = mutableMapOf(), var prefixCount: Int = 0)\n\n    private val root = TrieNode()\n\n    fun prefixCount(words: Array<String>, prefix: String): Int {\n        words.forEach { word ->\n            word.fold(root) { node, ch ->\n                node.children.getOrPut(ch) { TrieNode() }.apply { prefixCount++ }\n            }\n        }\n        return prefixSearch(prefix)?.prefixCount ?: 0\n    }\n\n    private fun prefixSearch(prefix: String): TrieNode? ## DesignAddAndSearchWordDataStructure

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/trie/DesignAddAndSearchWordDataStructure.kt`

## LongestCommonPrefix

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/trie/LongestCommonPrefix.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package string\n\nclass LongestCommonPrefix {\n    fun longestCommonPrefix(strs: Array<String>): String {\n        if (strs.isEmpty()) return \"\"\n\n        // Use the first string as the reference\n        for (i in strs[0].indices) {\n            val char = strs[0][i]\n            // Compare this character with the corresponding character in all other strings\n            for (j in 1 until strs.size) {\n                // If the current string is shorter or the characters don't match, return the prefix so far\n                if (i >= strs[j].length || strs[j][i] != char) {\n                    return strs[0].substring(0, i)\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        // If no mismatch is found, the entire first string is the common prefix\n        return strs[0]\n    }\n}"  java="class LongestCommonPrefix {\n    public static void $1(strs: Array<String>) {\n        if (strs.isEmpty()) return \"\"\n\n        // Use the strs[j][i] != char) {\n                    return strs[0].substring(0, i)\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        // If no mismatch is found, the entire first string is the common prefix\n        return strs[0]\n    }\n}"  python="class LongestCommonPrefix {\n    def $1(strs: Array<String>): str {\n        if (strs.isEmpty()) return \"\"\n\n        // Use the first string as }\n}"  rust="class LongestCommonPrefix {\n    fn $1(strs: Array<String>) -> String {\n        if (strs.isEmpty()) return \"\"\n\n        // Use the first string as the reference\n        for (i in strs[0].indices) {\n            val char = strs[0][i]\n            // Compare this character with the corresponding character in all other strings\n            for (j in 1 until strs.size) {\n ## SearchSuggestionSystem

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/trie/SearchSuggestionSystem.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package trie\n\nimport java.lang.StringBuilder\nimport java.util.*\n\n\nclass Trie {\n    data class TrieNode(\n        var ch: Char='*',\n        var isWord: Boolean = false,\n        var children: TreeMap<Char, TrieNode> = TreeMap()\n    )\n\n    val root = TrieNode()\n\n    fun insert(word: String) {\n        var currentNode = root\n\n        word.forEach { ch->  currentNode = currentNode.children.getOrPut(ch){ TrieNode(ch) } }\n\n        currentNode.isWord = true\n    }\n\n    fun search(word: String): List<String> {\n        val results = mutableListOf<String>()\n        var currentNode = root\n\n        word.forEach { ch -> currentNode = currentNode.children[ch] ?: return results }\n        // If we reach here, currentNode represents the node ending at 'word'\n        // Collect all words from this node downwards\n        collectWords(currentNode, word, results)\n\n        return results\n    }\n\n    fun collectWords(node: TrieNode?, prefix: String, results: MutableList<String>) {\n        if (node == null)\n            return\n        if (node.isWord)\n            results.add(prefix)\n\n        for((ch, childNode) in node.children) {\n            collectWords(childNode, prefix + ch, results)\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nclass SearchSuggestionSystem {\n    fun suggestedProducts(products: Array<String>, searchWord: String): List<List<String>> {\n        val trie = Trie()\n        val result = mutableListOf<List<String>>()\n        val prefixSearchString = StringBuilder()\n\n        products.forEach { trie.insert(it) }\n\n        searchWord.forEach { ch ->\n            prefixSearchString.append(ch)\n            result.add(trie.search(prefixSearchString.toString()).take(3))\n        }\n\n        return  result\n    }\n}"  java="class Trie {\n    data class TrieNode(\n        var ch: Char='*',\n        var isWord = false,\n        var children: TreeMap<Char, TrieNode> = ## WordBreak_I

Source: `/Users/arpanpathak/Projects/data_science/CrackGoogle/bin/main/trie/WordBreak_I.kt`

{% include code-tabs.html  kotlin="package trie\n\nclass WordBreak_I {\n    // TrieNode class as a data class\n    data class TrieNode(val children: MutableMap<Char, TrieNode> = mutableMapOf(), var endOfWord: Boolean = false)\n\n    fun wordBreak(s: String, wordDict: List<String>): Boolean {\n        val root = TrieNode()\n\n        // Build the Trie from the word dictionary\n        wordDict.forEach { word ->\n            var node = root\n            word.forEach { char ->\n                node = node.children.getOrPut(char) { TrieNode() }\n            }\n            node.endOfWord = true\n        }\n\n        val dp = mutableMapOf<Int, Boolean>().apply  { this[s.length] = true} // Base case: empty suffix can always be segmented\n\n        // Recursive function to check if string s[i..] can be segmented\n        fun canSegment(i: Int): Boolean {\n            dp[i]?.let {  return it }// Already marked as segmentable\n            var node = root\n\n            for (j in i until s.length) {\n                node = node.children[s[j]] ?: break // No match found for this character\n\n                when {\n                    node.endOfWord && canSegment(j + 1) -> return true.also { dp[i] = it }\n                }\n            }\n            return false.also { dp[i] = it }\n        }\n\n        return canSegment(0) // Start from the first character of the string\n    }\n}\n"  java="class WordBreak_I {\n    // TrieNode class as a data class\n    data class TrieNode(val children: MutableMap<Char, TrieNode> = mutableMapOf(), var endOfWord = false)\n\n
